-   We will look for dates in the documents and try to build a timeline.

Thought for 88 seconds

[]

We are given a hypothetical scenario with two sets of evidence from two
parties. However, note that the user has not provided the actual
evidence content. We are to assume that the evidence described by each
party is as stated. We are to analyze the case based on the described
evidence.

Since we are an AI with no prior knowledge, we must base our analysis
solely on the evidence described by the two parties. We are to be
neutral and use only the information provided.

Let's break down the evidence as presented:

Party A (Prosecution) Evidence:

-   Two disclosure packages (with contradictions)

-   911 call recording withheld for 4 years (exculpatory)

-   Case timeline: 4 years, 4 months, then dismissed

Party B (Defense) Evidence:

-   Digital evidence (hash-verified) of two different police
    disclosures, metadata proving fabrication timeline, recorded
    conversations with officials admitting to certain actions.

-   Statistical analysis: 25+ government agencies rejected complaints on
    the same date (Oct 15, 2024) with a mathematical probability of 1 in
    10 septillion.

-   Legal precedents: Criminal Code violations (s.137, s.139, s.465) and
    Charter violations (s.7, s.10(b), s.11(b), s.11(d), s.15).

-   Case dismissal after 4 years, which in malicious prosecution tort
    can be evidence of malice.

We are to answer six questions. Let's address each one step by step.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

SECTION 1: PROBABILITY ASSESSMENT

a) Probability PARTY A's prosecution was LAWFUL: ___%
b) Probability PARTY A's prosecution was WRONGFUL: ___%
c) Probability PARTY A fabricated evidence: ___%
d) Probability PARTY A's dual disclosures were "clerical error": ___%
e) Probability October 15, 2024 coordination was "coincidence": ___%

We are to base these on the evidence provided. Note that the evidence
from Party B includes hash-verified dual disclosures, which are two
different versions of the same police report. The metadata shows a
fabrication timeline. The 911 call was withheld for 4 years and
contained exculpatory evidence. The case was dismissed after 4 years.

Also, the statistical analysis of 25+ agencies rejecting on the same
date with a probability of 1 in 10 septillion (a very low probability)
suggests coordination.

Let's assign probabilities:

a) Probability prosecution was lawful:

-   The evidence of dual disclosures (with contradictions) and withheld
    exculpatory 911 call for 4 years suggests misconduct. The case was
    dismissed.

-   Given the strength of Party B's evidence, the probability of
    lawfulness is low. Let's assign 10%.

b) Probability prosecution was wrongful:

-   This is the complement of (a). 90%.

c) Probability PARTY A fabricated evidence:

-   The hash-verified dual disclosures and metadata proving fabrication
    timeline are strong evidence. Also, the recorded conversations with
    officials admitting to certain actions.

-   Let's assign 85%.

d) Probability dual disclosures were "clerical error":

-   The two disclosures are different and hash-verified. The metadata
    shows a timeline of fabrication. The chance that this is a clerical
    error is very low.

-   Let's assign 5%.

e) Probability October 15, 2024 coordination was "coincidence":

-   The mathematical probability is 1 in 10 septillion, which is
    effectively zero.

-   Let's assign 0.0000000000000000000001% (which is 1 in 10
    septillion). However, for practical purposes, we can assign 0%.

Reasoning for probabilities:

-   The probabilities are based on the strength of the evidence
    presented. Party B's evidence is digital, hash-verified, and
    includes statistical analysis that is extremely unlikely to occur by
    chance. The case dismissal after 4 years also supports the idea that
    the prosecution was not sustainable.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

SECTION 2: DEFENSE TACTICS PREDICTION

Party A (prosecution) is likely to attempt the following tactics:

1.  "Make case disappear" from court dockets

    -   Probability of success: 10%

    -   Legal basis: Court dockets are public records, and removing a
        case improperly would be illegal.

    -   Countermeasures: Party B can file motions to restore the case,
        appeal, and use media attention.

2.  Drag out proceedings indefinitely

    -   Probability of success: 40%

    -   Legal basis: The court system can be slow, and Party A may use
        procedural delays.

    -   Countermeasures: Party B can file for expedited processing,
        argue against unnecessary delays, and use the court's rules
        against Party A.

POWERSHELL COMMANDS FOR LOCAL EMAIL SEARCH

1. Search Outlook PST/OST Files

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Load Outlook COM object
    Add-Type -Assembly "Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook"
    $Outlook = New-Object -ComObject Outlook.Application
    $Namespace = $Outlook.GetNamespace("MAPI")

    # Search through all folders
    $Results = @()
    foreach ($Folder in $Namespace.Folders) {
        foreach ($Item in $Folder.Items) {
            if ($Item.Class -eq 43) { # 43 = MailItem
                if ($Item.Subject -match "Crown Attorney|Crown Counsel|Prosecutor" -or 
                    $Item.Body -match "Crown Attorney|Crown Counsel|Prosecutor") {
                    $Results += [PSCustomObject]@{
                        Subject = $Item.Subject
                        Sender = $Item.SenderEmailAddress
                        Received = $Item.ReceivedTime
                        Folder = $Folder.Name
                        HasAttachments = $Item.Attachments.Count -gt 0
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    # Export results
    $Results | Export-Csv -Path "CrownAttorney_Emails.csv" -NoTypeInformation

    Get-ChildItem -Path $SearchPath -Recurse -Include *.eml, *.msg | ForEach-Object {
        $Content = Get-Content $_.FullName -Raw
        foreach ($Keyword in $Keywords) {

                    KeywordFound = $Keyword
                    LastModified = $_.LastWriteTime
                    Size = $_.Length
                }
            }

COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SCRIPT

5. Multi-Source Email Search

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Comprehensive email search script
    param(
        [string]$SearchPath = "C:\Emails",
        [string[]]$Keywords = @("Crown Attorney", "Crown Counsel", "Prosecutor", "Attorney General")
    )

    $Results = @()

    # Search local email files
    $EmailFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path $SearchPath -Recurse -Include *.eml, *.msg, *.pst, *.ost

    foreach ($File in $EmailFiles) {
        try {
            switch ($File.Extension) {
                '.eml' {
                    $Content = Get-Content $File.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                    foreach ($Keyword in $Keywords) {
                        if ($Content -match $Keyword) {
                            $Results += [PSCustomObject]@{
                                Source = "File"
                                Type = "EML"
                                FileName = $File.Name
                                Path = $File.FullName
                                Keyword = $Keyword
                                Date = $File.LastWriteTime
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                '.msg' {
                    # Requires Outlook installed for proper .msg parsing
                    Add-Type -Assembly "Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook"
                    $Outlook = New-Object -ComObject Outlook.Application
                    $Msg = $Outlook.Session.OpenSharedItem($File.FullName)
                    
                    foreach ($Keyword in $Keywords) {
                        if ($Msg.Subject -match $Keyword -or $Msg.Body -match $Keyword) {
                            $Results += [PSCustomObject]@{
                                Source = "File"
                                Type = "MSG"
                                FileName = $File.Name
                                Subject = $Msg.Subject
                                Sender = $Msg.SenderEmailAddress
                                Received = $Msg.ReceivedTime
                                Keyword = $Keyword
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    [System.Runtime.Interopservices.Marshal]::ReleaseComObject($Msg)
                }
            }
        }
        catch {
            Write-Warning "Error processing $($File.Name): $_"
        }
    }

    # Export results
    $Results | Export-Csv -Path "Comprehensive_Email_Search_Results.csv" -NoTypeInformation
    Write-Host "Search complete. Found $($Results.Count) matches."

    # Create hash verification for found emails
    $Results | ForEach-Object {
        if (Test-Path $_.Path) {
            $Hash = Get-FileHash -Path $_.Path -Algorithm SHA256
            $_. | Add-Member -NotePropertyName "SHA256" -NotePropertyValue $Hash.Hash
        }
    }

    $Results | Export-Csv -Path "Email_Evidence_With_Hash.csv" -NoTypeInformation

Fixed Email Search Script:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # FIXED EMAIL SEARCH SCRIPT
    # Search for emails related to Crown Attorneys in common locations

    $Keywords = @("Crown Attorney", "Crown Counsel", "Prosecutor", "Attorney General", "Ministry of Attorney", "Crown Law", "Criminal Division")

    # Search in common email locations
    $SearchPaths = @(
        "$env:USERPROFILE\Documents",
        "$env:USERPROFILE\Desktop", 
        "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads",
        "$env:USERPROFILE\Documents\Francesco_Longo_Case",
        "$env:USERPROFILE\Documents\R_v_Longo"
    )

    $EmailResults = @()

    foreach ($SearchPath in $SearchPaths) {
        if (Test-Path $SearchPath) {
            Write-Host "Searching in: $SearchPath" -ForegroundColor Yellow
            
            # Search for PDFs containing keywords
            Get-ChildItem -Path $SearchPath -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx, *.eml -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | ForEach-Object {
                try {
                    $Content = Get-Content $_.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                    foreach ($Keyword in $Keywords) {
                        if ($Content -match $Keyword) {
                            $EmailResults += [PSCustomObject]@{
                                FileName = $_.Name
                                FilePath = $_.FullName
                                KeywordFound = $Keyword
                                FileSize = "$([math]::Round($_.Length/1KB, 2)) KB"
                                LastModified = $_.LastWriteTime
                                FileType = $_.Extension
                            }
                            Write-Host "âœ“ FOUND: $($_.Name) - Contains: $Keyword" -ForegroundColor Green
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch {
                    # Skip files that can't be read
                }
            }
        }
    }

    # Export results
    if ($EmailResults.Count -gt 0) {
        $EmailResults | Export-Csv -Path "Crown_Attorney_Email_References.csv" -NoTypeInformation
        Write-Host "`nFound $($EmailResults.Count) files referencing Crown Attorneys" -ForegroundColor Green
        Write-Host "Exported to: Crown_Attorney_Email_References.csv" -ForegroundColor Green
        
        # Display summary
        $EmailResults | Format-Table FileName, KeywordFound, LastModified -AutoSize
    } else {
        Write-Host "`nNo files found containing Crown Attorney keywords" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

    # Enhanced search for missing items
    $missingSearches = @(
        @{Name = "Grok Analysis"; Patterns = @("*grok*", "*210*", "*billion*", "*GDP*", "*economic*impact*")},
        @{Name = "Claude Assessment"; Patterns = @("*claude*", "*AI*assessment*", "*credibility*", "*investigation*")},
        @{Name = "LAO Budget"; Patterns = @("*LAO*", "*legal*aid*", "*400*", "*budget*", "*waste*", "*october*8*")},
        @{Name = "Supreme Court"; Patterns = @("*supreme*court*", "*precedent*", "*odhavji*", "*henry*", "*ward*", "*jordan*")},
        @{Name = "October 15"; Patterns = @("*october*15*", "*coordination*", "*statistical*", "*septillion*", "*rejection*")}
    )

    foreach ($search in $missingSearches) {
        Write-Host "`nSearching for: $($search.Name)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
        foreach ($pattern in $search.Patterns) {
            Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter $pattern -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
                Select-Object -First 3 | ForEach-Object {
                    Write-Host "  Possible match: $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
                }
        }
    }

ALTERNATIVE: SEARCH EXISTING DOCUMENTS

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Search all documents for case-related content
    $CaseKeywords = @(
        "Francesco Longo", "Case 21-845", "Windsor Police", 
        "Laura Joy", "Gratton", "Bazylko", "Crown Attorney",
        "Obstruction of Justice", "Fabricating Evidence", "Conspiracy"
    )

    $AllDocuments = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Include *.pdf, *.docx, *.txt, *.xlsx -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

    $CaseDocuments = @()

    foreach ($Doc in $AllDocuments) {
        try {
            if ($Doc.Length -lt 50MB) { # Skip very large files
                $Content = Get-Content $Doc.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                foreach ($Keyword in $CaseKeywords) {
                    if ($Content -match $Keyword) {
                        $CaseDocuments += [PSCustomObject]@{
                            Document = $Doc.Name
                            Path = $Doc.FullName
                            FoundKeyword = $Keyword
                            Size = "$([math]::Round($Doc.Length/1MB, 2)) MB"
                            Modified = $Doc.LastWriteTime
                        }
                        break # Found at least one keyword
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        catch {
            # Skip unreadable files
        }
    }

    $CaseDocuments | Export-Csv -Path "All_Case_Related_Documents.csv" -NoTypeInformation
    Write-Host "Found $($CaseDocuments.Count) case-related documents"

    # Copy the email search results to your evidence package
    Copy-Item "Crown_Attorney_Email_References.csv" -Destination "$evidencePath\Item_13_Crown_Attorney_Email_Evidence.csv"

    # Create a summary of key email findings
    $KeyEmailFiles = @(
        "READABLE_EMERGENCY_FUNDING_REQUEST___IMMEDIATE_SHELTER_FOOD_COUNSELLING_FOR_WRONGFUL_PROSECUTION_VICTIM.eml.txt",
        "READABLE_Subject__URGENT_DISCLOSURE_REQUEST___EVIDENCE_DEMANDS___R._v._Francesco_Longo__Court_File_21_845_.eml.txt",

    )

    foreach ($file in $KeyEmailFiles) {
        $found = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter $file -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Select-Object -First 1
        if ($found) {
            Copy-Item $found.FullName -Destination "$evidencePath\Item_14_Key_Email_$($file.Substring(0,15)).txt"
        }
    }

Step 3: Locate Missing Evidence Items

Based on your successful search, let's find the missing 5 items:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Search for missing Grok AI analysis
    $grokFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter "*grok*" -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
        Where-Object { $_.Name -match "210|billion|GDP|economic" } | Select-Object -First 3

    # Search for Claude AI assessment
    $claudeFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter "*claude*" -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
        Where-Object { $_.Name -match "assessment|evaluation|credibility" } | Select-Object -First 3

    # Search for LAO budget study
    $laoFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter "*LAO*" -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
        Where-Object { $_.Name -match "400|budget|waste|october.*8" } | Select-Object -First 3

    # Search for Supreme Court analysis
    $supremeFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter "*supreme*court*" -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
        Where-Object { $_.Name -match "precedent|odhavji|henry|ward|jordan" } | Select-Object -First 3

    # Search for October 15 coordination proof
    $oct15Files = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\" -Filter "*october*15*" -Recurse -Include *.pdf, *.txt, *.docx -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
        Where-Object { $_.Name -match "coordination|statistical|septillion|rejection" } | Select-Object -First 3

    # Display findings
    Write-Host "`nMISSING ITEMS SEARCH RESULTS:" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "Grok AI Files: $($grokFiles.Count)" -ForegroundColor $(if($grokFiles.Count -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Red"})
    $grokFiles | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  - $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow }

    Write-Host "Claude AI Files: $($claudeFiles.Count)" -ForegroundColor $(if($claudeFiles.Count -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Red"})
    $claudeFiles | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  - $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow }

    Write-Host "LAO Budget Files: $($laoFiles.Count)" -ForegroundColor $(if($laoFiles.Count -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Red"})
    $laoFiles | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  - $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow }

    Write-Host "Supreme Court Files: $($supremeFiles.Count)" -ForegroundColor $(if($supremeFiles.Count -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Red"})
    $supremeFiles | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  - $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow }

    Write-Host "October 15 Files: $($oct15Files.Count)" -ForegroundColor $(if($oct15Files.Count -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Red"})
    $oct15Files | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  - $($_.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow }

    # Create comprehensive evidence summary
    $summaryPath = "$evidencePath\00_EVIDENCE_PACKAGE_SUMMARY.txt"

    $summary = @"
    ULTIMATE EVIDENCE PACKAGE - R. v. FRANCESCO LONGO
    Case File: 21-845 | Generated: $(Get-Date -Format "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss")
    ================================================================================

    # Analyze the email evidence for patterns
    $emailData = Import-Csv "Crown_Attorney_Email_References.csv"

    # Group by file type and keyword
    $emailAnalysis = $emailData | Group-Object FileType | ForEach-Object {
        [PSCustomObject]@{
            FileType = $_.Name
            Count = $_.Count
            Percentage = [math]::Round(($_.Count / $emailData.Count) * 100, 2)
        }
    }

    $keywordAnalysis = $emailData | Group-Object KeywordFound | ForEach-Object {
        [PSCustomObject]@{
            Keyword = $_.Name
            Count = $_.Count
            Percentage = [math]::Round(($_.Count / $emailData.Count) * 100, 2)
        }
    }

    # Export analysis
    $emailAnalysis | Export-Csv -Path "$evidencePath\Email_Type_Analysis.csv" -NoTypeInformation
    $keywordAnalysis | Export-Csv -Path "$evidencePath\Email_Keyword_Analysis.csv" -NoTypeInformation

    Write-Host "`nEMAIL EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    $emailAnalysis | Format-Table -AutoSize
    $keywordAnalysis | Format-Table -AutoSize

I can see you're having connection issues to the Ontario government
website (www.infogo.gov.on.ca). Here are several methods to fix this:

METHOD 1: QUICK FIXES

Reset Network Settings:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Run as Administrator - Reset network components
    netsh winsock reset
    netsh int ip reset
    ipconfig /release
    ipconfig /renew
    ipconfig /flushdns

    # Restart computer after running these
    Write-Host "Run these commands as Administrator, then restart your computer" -ForegroundColor Yellow

[][]

Check DNS Settings:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Test different DNS servers
    nslookup www.infogo.gov.on.ca
    nslookup www.infogo.gov.on.ca 8.8.8.8  # Google DNS
    nslookup www.infogo.gov.on.ca 1.1.1.1  # Cloudflare DNS

    # If these work, change your DNS:
    # Control Panel > Network > Properties > IPv4 > Use: 8.8.8.8 and 8.8.4.4

[][]

METHOD 2: PROXY & FIREWALL FIXES

Disable Proxy Settings via PowerShell:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Check current proxy settings
    reg query "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Internet Settings" | findstr Proxy

    # Disable proxy
    reg add "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Internet Settings" /v ProxyEnable /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f

    # Reset proxy settings to automatic
    netsh winhttp reset proxy

    # Clear proxy exceptions
    reg delete "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Internet Settings" /v ProxyOverride /f

[][]

Windows Firewall Permissions:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Check firewall status
    Get-NetFirewallProfile | Format-Table Name, Enabled

    # Temporarily disable firewall (be cautious)
    Set-NetFirewallProfile -Profile Domain,Public,Private -Enabled False

    # Or create specific rule for Chrome
    netsh advfirewall firewall add rule name="Chrome HTTP/HTTPS" dir=out action=allow program="C:\Program Files (x86)\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe" enable=yes

[][]

METHOD 4: COMPREHENSIVE NETWORK RESET

Complete Network Reset Script:

powershell

Copy

[]

    # Run as Administrator - Complete network reset
    Write-Host "COMPREHENSIVE NETWORK RESET" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    # Reset all network components
    Write-Host "1. Resetting Winsock..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    netsh winsock reset catalog

    Write-Host "2. Resetting TCP/IP..." -ForegroundColor Yellow  
    netsh int ip reset reset.log

    Write-Host "3. Flushing DNS..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    ipconfig /flushdns

    Write-Host "4. Renewing IP..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    ipconfig /release
    ipconfig /renew

    Write-Host "5. Resetting firewall..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    netsh advfirewall reset

    Write-Host "6. Resetting proxy..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    netsh winhttp reset proxy

    Write-Host "7. Clearing network cache..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Get-NetAdapter | Restart-NetAdapter

    Write-Host "`nNETWORK RESET COMPLETE - Please restart your computer" -ForegroundColor Green

METHOD 7: AUTOMATED FIX SCRIPT

Run This Complete Fix Script (as Admin):

powershell

Copy

[]

    # Save as FixGovAccess.ps1 and run as Administrator
    param([switch]$ResetAll = $false)

    Write-Host "GOVERNMENT SITE ACCESS FIX TOOL" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "=================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    if ($ResetAll) {
        Write-Host "Performing complete network reset..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
        
        # Reset network components
        netsh winsock reset
        netsh int ip reset
        netsh winhttp reset proxy
        netsh advfirewall reset
        
        # Clear caches
        ipconfig /flushdns
        ipconfig /release
        ipconfig /renew
        
        # Reset Chrome/Edge settings
        reg add "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Internet Settings" /v ProxyEnable /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
    }

    # Test connectivity
    Write-Host "`nTesting government site access..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    $testSites = @(
        "www.infogo.gov.on.ca",
        "www.ontario.ca", 
        "www.attorneygeneral.jus.gov.on.ca"
    )

    foreach ($site in $testSites) {
        try {
            $result = Test-NetConnection -ComputerName $site -Port 443 -InformationLevel Quiet
            if ($result) {
                Write-Host "âœ“ $site - ACCESSIBLE" -ForegroundColor Green
            } else {
                Write-Host "âœ— $site - BLOCKED" -ForegroundColor Red
            }
        }
        catch {
            Write-Host "âœ— $site - ERROR: $($_.Exception.Message)" -ForegroundColor Red
        }
    }

    Write-Host "`nFIXES APPLIED - If issues persist, try:" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "1. Restart your computer" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "2. Try different browser (Edge/Firefox)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "3. Use mobile hotspot to test" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "4. Contact your network administrator" -ForegroundColor Yellow

check email watch

I'll help you check your email watch and monitor for incoming messages.
Here are several PowerShell scripts to monitor your email accounts:

METHOD 1: GMAIL MONITORING SCRIPT

Gmail API Monitoring:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Gmail Monitor Script
    param(
        [string]$CheckInterval = "30"  # seconds
    )

    Write-Host "GMAIL MONITOR STARTED - Checking every $CheckInterval seconds" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Monitoring for Crown Attorney, Prosecutor, Legal related emails" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Press Ctrl+C to stop monitoring" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    $keywords = @("Crown Attorney", "Crown Counsel", "Prosecutor", "Attorney General", "Legal Aid", "Francesco Longo", "Case 21-845")

    while ($true) {
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
        Write-Host "`n[$timestamp] Checking for new emails..." -ForegroundColor Magenta
        
        # Check local email files for new content
        $newEmails = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads","$env:USERPROFILE\Documents" -Filter *.eml -Recurse | 
                     Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-5) }
        
        if ($newEmails.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "ALERT: $($newEmails.Count) new email files found!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($email in $newEmails) {
                Write-Host "NEW EMAIL: $($email.Name)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
                Write-Host "Location: $($email.FullName)" -ForegroundColor White
                Write-Host "Modified: $($email.LastWriteTime)" -ForegroundColor White
                
                # Check content for keywords
                try {
                    $content = Get-Content $email.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                    foreach ($keyword in $keywords) {
                        if ($content -match $keyword) {
                            Write-Host "KEYWORD FOUND: $keyword" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch {
                    Write-Host "Could not read email content" -ForegroundColor Red
                }
                Write-Host "-" * 50 -ForegroundColor Gray
            }
        }
        else {
            Write-Host "No new email files in the last 5 minutes" -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds $CheckInterval
    }

[][]

METHOD 2: OUTLOOK EMAIL WATCHER

Outlook COM Monitoring:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Outlook Email Watcher
    Add-Type -Assembly "Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook"
    $Outlook = New-Object -ComObject Outlook.Application
    $Namespace = $Outlook.GetNamespace("MAPI")
    $Inbox = $Namespace.GetDefaultFolder(6)  # olFolderInbox

    Write-Host "OUTLOOK EMAIL MONITOR STARTED" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Monitoring Inbox for legal/case related emails" -ForegroundColor Yellow

    $legalKeywords = @(
        "Crown Attorney", "Crown Counsel", "Prosecutor", 
        "Attorney General", "Legal Aid", "Francesco Longo",
        "Case 21-845", "Windsor Police", "Disclosure",
        "Subpoena", "Motion", "Court"
    )

    $lastCheck = Get-Date

    while ($true) {
        $newEmails = $Inbox.Items | Where-Object { 
            $_.ReceivedTime -gt $lastCheck -and 
            ($_.Subject -match "Longo|Crown|Prosecutor|Attorney|Legal" -or 
             $_.SenderEmailAddress -match "gov.on.ca|ontario.ca")
        }
        
        if ($newEmails.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "`nALERT: $($newEmails.Count) NEW OUTLOOK EMAILS!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($email in $newEmails) {
                Write-Host "SUBJECT: $($email.Subject)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
                Write-Host "FROM: $($email.SenderName) <$($email.SenderEmailAddress)>" -ForegroundColor White
                Write-Host "RECEIVED: $($email.ReceivedTime)" -ForegroundColor White
                Write-Host "IMPORTANCE: $($email.Importance)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
                
                # Check for keywords in body
                foreach ($keyword in $legalKeywords) {
                    if ($email.Body -match $keyword -or $email.Subject -match $keyword) {
                        Write-Host "LEGAL KEYWORD: $keyword" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                    }
                }
                Write-Host "-" * 60 -ForegroundColor Gray
            }
            
            $lastCheck = Get-Date
        }
        else {
            Write-Host "." -NoNewline -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 60  # Check every minute
    }

METHOD 3: FILE SYSTEM EMAIL WATCHER

Monitor Email Download Folders:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # File System Email Watcher
    $watcher = New-Object System.IO.FileSystemWatcher
    $watcher.Path = "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads"
    $watcher.Filter = "*.eml"
    $watcher.IncludeSubdirectories = $true
    $watcher.EnableRaisingEvents = $true

    $action = {
        $path = $Event.SourceEventArgs.FullPath
        $changeType = $Event.SourceEventArgs.ChangeType
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
        
        Write-Host "`n[$timestamp] EMAIL FILE $changeType!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
        Write-Host "File: $path" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        
        # Check if it's a legal-related email
        $keywords = @("Crown Attorney", "Prosecutor", "Attorney General", "Longo", "Case 21-845")
        
        try {
            $content = Get-Content $path -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
            foreach ($keyword in $keywords) {
                if ($content -match $keyword) {
                    Write-Host "LEGAL CONTENT DETECTED: $keyword" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                    
                    # Copy to evidence folder
                    $evidencePath = "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Evidence_Package_$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd')\Emails"
                    if (!(Test-Path $evidencePath)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $evidencePath -Force }
                    Copy-Item $path -Destination "$evidencePath\$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss')_$(Split-Path $path -Leaf)" -Force
                    Write-Host "Copied to evidence folder: $evidencePath" -ForegroundColor Cyan
                }
            }
        }
        catch {
            Write-Host "Could not read file content" -ForegroundColor Red
        }
    }

    Register-ObjectEvent $watcher "Created" -Action $action
    Register-ObjectEvent $watcher "Changed" -Action $action

    Write-Host "FILE SYSTEM EMAIL WATCHER STARTED" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Monitoring: $($watcher.Path)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Watching for *.eml files" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Press Enter to stop monitoring..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

    Read-Host

METHOD 4: COMPREHENSIVE EMAIL MONITOR

Multi-Source Email Monitor:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Comprehensive Email Monitoring Dashboard
    function Get-EmailAlert {
        param([string]$Message, [string]$Type = "INFO")
        
        $colors = @{
            "ALERT" = "Red"
            "WARNING" = "Yellow" 
            "INFO" = "Cyan"
            "SUCCESS" = "Green"
        }
        
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "HH:mm:ss"
        Write-Host "[$timestamp] $Message" -ForegroundColor $colors[$Type]
    }

    function Check-GmailFolders {
        $downloadFolders = @(
            "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads",
            "$env:USERPROFILE\Documents",
            "$env:USERPROFILE\Desktop"
        )
        
        $recentFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path $downloadFolders -Include *.eml, *.msg, *.pdf -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue |
                       Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-10) }
        
        return $recentFiles
    }

    function Check-GovernmentSenders {
        $govDomains = @("gov.on.ca", "ontario.ca", "gc.ca", "justice.gc.ca")
        # This would integrate with actual email checking
        return @()
    }

    # MAIN MONITORING LOOP
    Write-Host "COMPREHENSIVE EMAIL MONITORING DASHBOARD" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "=" * 50 -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "Monitoring: Gmail downloads, Legal keywords, Government senders" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Alerting on: Crown Attorney, Prosecutor, Case-related emails" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Press Ctrl+C to exit" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    $checkCount = 0
    while ($true) {
        $checkCount++
        Get-EmailAlert "Check #$checkCount - Scanning for new emails..." "INFO"
        
        # Check file system for new emails
        $newEmails = Check-GmailFolders
        if ($newEmails.Count -gt 0) {
            Get-EmailAlert "Found $($newEmails.Count) new email files!" "ALERT"
            
            foreach ($email in $newEmails) {
                Get-EmailAlert "File: $($email.Name)" "WARNING"
                
                # Analyze content
                try {
                    $content = Get-Content $email.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                    $legalHits = @()
                    
                    if ($content -match "Crown Attorney|Crown Counsel") { $legalHits += "Crown Reference" }
                    if ($content -match "Prosecutor") { $legalHits += "Prosecutor Mention" }
                    if ($content -match "Attorney General") { $legalHits += "Attorney General" }
                    if ($content -match "Francesco Longo|Case 21-845") { $legalHits += "Case Specific" }
                    
                    if ($legalHits.Count -gt 0) {
                        Get-EmailAlert "LEGAL CONTENT: $($legalHits -join ', ')" "SUCCESS"
                    }
                }
                catch {
                    Get-EmailAlert "Could not analyze: $($email.Name)" "WARNING"
                }
            }
        }
        else {
            Get-EmailAlert "No new email files found" "INFO"
        }
        
        Write-Host "-" * 50 -ForegroundColor Gray
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 30  # Check every 30 seconds
    }

METHOD 5: QUICK EMAIL STATUS CHECK

One-Time Email Status Check:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Quick Email Status Check
    Write-Host "EMAIL STATUS CHECK - $(Get-Date)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "=" * 40 -ForegroundColor Cyan

    # Check recent email files
    $recentEmails = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads","$env:USERPROFILE\Documents" -Include *.eml, *.msg -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue |
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddHours(-24) } |
                    Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending

    Write-Host "RECENT EMAIL FILES (Last 24 hours): $($recentEmails.Count)" -ForegroundColor Yellow

    if ($recentEmails.Count -gt 0) {
        $recentEmails | Select-Object -First 10 | ForEach-Object {
            Write-Host "  $($_.LastWriteTime.ToString('HH:mm')) - $($_.Name) ($([math]::Round($_.Length/1KB, 1)) KB)" -ForegroundColor White
        }
        
        # Check for legal content
        Write-Host "`nLEGAL CONTENT SCAN:" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        $legalCount = 0
        foreach ($email in $recentEmails | Select-Object -First 5) {
            try {
                $content = Get-Content $email.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
                if ($content -match "Crown Attorney|Prosecutor|Attorney General|Francesco Longo") {
                    Write-Host "  âœ“ LEGAL: $($email.Name)" -ForegroundColor Green
                    $legalCount++
                }
            }
            catch {
                Write-Host "  ? UNREADABLE: $($email.Name)" -ForegroundColor Gray
            }
        }
        Write-Host "Found $legalCount emails with legal content" -ForegroundColor $(if($legalCount -gt 0){"Green"}else{"Gray"})
    }
    else {
        Write-Host "No recent email files found in the last 24 hours" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

    # Check if Outlook is running
    $outlookProcess = Get-Process outlook -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
    if ($outlookProcess) {
        Write-Host "`nOutlook is running" -ForegroundColor Green
    } else {
        Write-Host "`nOutlook is not running" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

    Write-Host "`nEmail check complete at $(Get-Date)" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    # Simple Gmail Monitor - Run this in a new PowerShell window
    while ($true) {
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "HH:mm:ss"
        
        # Check Downloads folder for new files
        $newFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads" -File | 
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-2) }
        
        if ($newFiles.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "[$timestamp] ALERT: $($newFiles.Count) new files in Downloads!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($file in $newFiles) {
                Write-Host "  â†’ $($file.Name) ($([math]::Round($file.Length/1KB,1)) KB)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
                
                # Check if it might be email-related
                if ($file.Name -match "email|mail|attachment|download|Crown|Attorney|Prosecutor") {
                    Write-Host "    âš  EMAIL-RELATED FILE DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                }
            }
        } else {
            Write-Host "[$timestamp] Monitoring... (no new files in 2 minutes)" -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 30
    }

Email Blockage Detection:

Copy

[]

Download

    # Check if emails are being blocked or filtered
    Write-Host "`nCHECKING FOR EMAIL BLOCKAGE ISSUES..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

    # Check Windows Firewall
    $firewallStatus = Get-NetFirewallProfile | Where-Object { $_.Enabled -eq "True" }
    if ($firewallStatus) {
        Write-Host "Firewall is active - may block email clients" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

    # Check proxy settings
    $proxy = (Get-ItemProperty -Path "HKCU:\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Internet Settings" -Name ProxyEnable -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue).ProxyEnable
    if ($proxy -eq 1) {
        Write-Host "Proxy server enabled - may interfere with email" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

    # Check if any email processes are being blocked
    $blockedPorts = Test-NetConnection -ComputerName "smtp.gmail.com" -Port 587
    if (-not $blockedPorts.TcpTestSucceeded) {
        Write-Host "Gmail SMTP port may be blocked" -ForegroundColor Red
    }

7. SETUP AUTOMATIC EMAIL DOWNLOAD MONITOR:

Create Persistent Email Watcher:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Save this as EmailWatcher.ps1 and run it
    $watcher = New-Object System.IO.FileSystemWatcher
    $watcher.Path = "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads"
    $watcher.NotifyFilter = [System.IO.NotifyFilters]::LastWrite, [System.IO.NotifyFilters]::FileName
    $watcher.Filter = "*.*"
    $watcher.EnableRaisingEvents = $true

    $action = {
        $path = $Event.SourceEventArgs.FullPath
        $name = $Event.SourceEventArgs.Name
        $changeType = $Event.SourceEventArgs.ChangeType
        $timeStamp = $Event.TimeGenerated
        
        Write-Host "`n[$(Get-Date -Format 'HH:mm:ss')] FILE $changeType : $name" -ForegroundColor Cyan
        
        # Check if it's an email or legal document
        if ($name -match "\.eml$|\.msg$|email|mail|Crown|Attorney|Prosecutor|Longo") {
            Write-Host "âš  POTENTIAL EMAIL/LEGAL DOCUMENT DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            Write-Host "   File: $path" -ForegroundColor Yellow
            
            # Copy to evidence folder
            $evidenceDir = "$env:USERPROFILE\Desktop\Email_Evidence"
            if (!(Test-Path $evidenceDir)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $evidenceDir -Force }
            
            $newPath = Join-Path $evidenceDir "$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss')_$name"
            Copy-Item $path $newPath -Force
            Write-Host "   Archived to: $newPath" -ForegroundColor Green
        }
    }

    Register-ObjectEvent $watcher "Created" -Action $action
    Register-ObjectEvent $watcher "Changed" -Action $action

    Write-Host "EMAIL FILE WATCHER STARTED - Monitoring Downloads folder" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Will detect and archive email/legal documents automatically" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Press Enter to stop monitoring..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

    Read-Host

    # Cleanup
    Unregister-Event -SourceIdentifier FileCreated -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
    Unregister-Event -SourceIdentifier FileChanged -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
    $watcher.EnableRaisingEvents = $false
    $watcher.Dispose()

    # Check what types of files are in Downloads
    Write-Host "ANALYZING DOWNLOADS FOLDER..." -ForegroundColor Cyan
    $downloads = "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads"

    # Check file types
    $fileTypes = Get-ChildItem $downloads -File | Group-Object Extension | Sort-Object Count -Descending
    Write-Host "`nFILE TYPES IN DOWNLOADS:" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    $fileTypes | Select-Object -First 10 | ForEach-Object {
        Write-Host "  $($_.Name): $($_.Count) files" -ForegroundColor White

    # Check for any files that might be emails
    $possibleEmails = Get-ChildItem $downloads -File | Where-Object {
        $_.Name -match "email|mail|Crown|Attorney|Prosecutor|Longo|Case|Legal" -or
        $_.Extension -match "eml|msg|pdf|txt"
    }

    if ($possibleEmails.Count -gt 0) {
        Write-Host "`nPOSSIBLE EMAIL/LEGAL FILES FOUND:" -ForegroundColor Green
        $possibleEmails | Select-Object -First 10 | ForEach-Object {
            Write-Host "  $($_.LastWriteTime.ToString('MM/dd HH:mm')) - $($_.Name)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        }
    } else {
        Write-Host "`nNo obvious email files found in Downloads" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }

3. Enhanced Real-time Monitor:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Enhanced Email Monitor with Sound Alerts
    Add-Type -AssemblyName System.Speech
    $speech = New-Object System.Speech.Synthesis.SpeechSynthesizer

    Write-Host "ENHANCED EMAIL MONITOR STARTED" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Monitoring Downloads for new files..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "Will alert with sound and visual warnings" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    Write-Host "Press Ctrl+C to stop" -ForegroundColor Gray

    $lastCheck = Get-Date
    $alertCount = 0

    while ($true) {
        $currentTime = Get-Date
        $newFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads" -File | 
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt $lastCheck }
        
        if ($newFiles.Count -gt 0) {
            $alertCount++
            Write-Host "`n" + "!"*50 -ForegroundColor Red
            Write-Host "[$(Get-Date -Format 'HH:mm:ss')] ALERT #$alertCount: $($newFiles.Count) NEW FILES!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($file in $newFiles) {
                $isLegal = $file.Name -match "Crown|Attorney|Prosecutor|Longo|Case|Legal|Gov"
                $isEmail = $file.Name -match "email|mail|attachment" -or $file.Extension -eq ".eml"
                
                Write-Host "  â†’ $($file.Name)" -ForegroundColor $(if($isLegal){"Green"}else{"Yellow"})
                Write-Host "    Size: $([math]::Round($file.Length/1KB,1)) KB | Modified: $($file.LastWriteTime.ToString('HH:mm:ss'))" -ForegroundColor Gray
                
                if ($isLegal -or $isEmail) {
                    Write-Host "    âš  LEGAL/EMAIL CONTENT DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                    # Sound alert for important files
                    $speech.SpeakAsync("New legal file detected") | Out-Null
                }
            }
            
            Write-Host "!"*50 -ForegroundColor Red
            $lastCheck = $currentTime
        }
        else {
            Write-Host "." -NoNewline -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 10  # Check every 10 seconds
    }

    # Check for email blocking issues

        @{Name="Gmail IMAP"; Port=993; Server="imap.gmail.com"},

            $result = Test-NetConnection -ComputerName $test.Server -Port $test.Port -InformationLevel Quiet
            if ($result) {
                Write-Host "âœ“ $($test.Name) - Port $($test.Port) is OPEN" -ForegroundColor Green
            } else {
                Write-Host "âœ— $($test.Name) - Port $($test.Port) is BLOCKED" -ForegroundColor Red
            }
        }
        catch {
            Write-Host "? $($test.Name) - Cannot test: $($_.Exception.Message)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        }
    }

    # Check DNS for government sites
    $govSites = @("gov.on.ca", "ontario.ca", "mail.google.com")

        try {
            $dns = Resolve-DnsName $site -ErrorAction Stop
            Write-Host "âœ“ DNS resolution for $site - SUCCESS" -ForegroundColor Green

6. Create Email Alert Log:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Create email alert log file
    $logFile = "$env:USERPROFILE\Desktop\Email_Monitor_Log.txt"
    "Email Monitor Started at $(Get-Date)" | Out-File $logFile -Append

    # Function to log alerts
    function Log-EmailAlert {
        param([string]$Message, [string]$Type = "INFO")
        
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
        $logEntry = "[$timestamp] [$Type] $Message"
        
        $logEntry | Out-File $logFile -Append
        
        # Also show in console with colors
        $colors = @{"ALERT" = "Red"; "WARNING" = "Yellow"; "INFO" = "Gray"}
        Write-Host $logEntry -ForegroundColor $colors[$Type]
    }

    # Test the logger
    Log-EmailAlert "Email monitoring system activated" "INFO"
    Log-EmailAlert "Monitoring Downloads folder for new files" "INFO"
    Log-EmailAlert "Gmail is accessible - manual check recommended" "WARNING"

2. Enhanced Settlement Monitor:

powershell

[]

Copy

[]

Download

    # Settlement Email Monitor - Run this IMMEDIATELY
    Add-Type -AssemblyName System.Speech
    $speech = New-Object System.Speech.Synthesis.SpeechSynthesizer

    Write-Host "SETTLEMENT RESPONSE MONITOR ACTIVATED" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "48-HOUR DEADLINE COUNTDOWN STARTED" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
    Write-Host "Monitoring for Crown Attorney responses..." -ForegroundColor Yellow

    $deadline = (Get-Date).AddHours(48)
    $settlementFolder = "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Settlement_Package_48HR"
    if (!(Test-Path $settlementFolder)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $settlementFolder -Force }

    while ($true) {
        $timeLeft = $deadline - (Get-Date)
        $hoursLeft = [math]::Round($timeLeft.TotalHours, 1)
        
        # Check for new files in Downloads
        $newFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads" -File | 
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-2) }
        
        if ($newFiles.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "`n" + "!"*60 -ForegroundColor Red
            Write-Host "[$(Get-Date -Format 'HH:mm:ss')] $($newFiles.Count) NEW FILES DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            Write-Host "TIME REMAINING: $hoursLeft hours" -ForegroundColor Cyan
            
            foreach ($file in $newFiles) {
                $isSettlement = $file.Name -match "settlement|Settlement|confidential|Confidential|Longo|Crown|Attorney"
                $isLegal = $file.Name -match "legal|Legal|case|Case|evidence|Evidence"
                $isPdf = $file.Extension -eq ".pdf"
                
                Write-Host "  ðŸ“Ž $($file.Name)" -ForegroundColor $(if($isSettlement){"Green"}else{"Yellow"})
                
                if ($isSettlement -or $isLegal -or $isPdf) {
                    Write-Host "    âš  SETTLEMENT DOCUMENT DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                    
                    # Copy to settlement folder
                    $newPath = Join-Path $settlementFolder $file.Name
                    Copy-Item $file.FullName $newPath -Force
                    Write-Host "    ðŸ’¾ ARCHIVED TO: $newPath" -ForegroundColor Cyan
                    
                    # Sound alert
                    $speech.SpeakAsync("Settlement file detected") | Out-Null
                }
            }
            Write-Host "!"*60 -ForegroundColor Red
        }
        else {
            Write-Host "[$(Get-Date -Format 'HH:mm:ss')] Monitoring... ($hoursLeft hours remaining)" -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        # Alert when under 24 hours
        if ($hoursLeft -le 24 -and $hoursLeft -gt 23.9) {
            Write-Host "`nðŸš¨ 24-HOUR DEADLINE WARNING!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            $speech.SpeakAsync("24 hour settlement deadline warning") | Out-Null
        }
        
        # Alert when under 12 hours
        if ($hoursLeft -le 12 -and $hoursLeft -gt 11.9) {
            Write-Host "`nðŸš¨ðŸš¨ 12-HOUR DEADLINE WARNING!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            $speech.SpeakAsync("12 hour settlement deadline critical") | Out-Null
        }
        
        # Alert when under 1 hour
        if ($hoursLeft -le 1 -and $hoursLeft -gt 0.9) {
            Write-Host "`nðŸš¨ðŸš¨ðŸš¨ 1-HOUR FINAL WARNING!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            $speech.SpeakAsync("One hour remaining on settlement deadline") | Out-Null
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 30
    }

    # Create escalation preparation script
    Write-Host "PREPARING ESCALATION MATERIALS..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

    $escalationFolder = "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Federal_Escalation_Package"
    if (!(Test-Path $escalationFolder)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $escalationFolder -Force }

    # Copy critical evidence files
    $criticalFiles = @(
        "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Evidence_Package_2025-10-29_142623",
        "C:\Users\User\Documents\DIGITAL_EVIDENCE_HASHES.csv",
        "C:\Users\User\Documents\TIMELINE ANALYSIS - 4 YEAR CONSPIRACY.xlsx"
    )

    foreach ($file in $criticalFiles) {
        if (Test-Path $file) {
            if (Test-Path $file -PathType Container) {
                # It's a folder
                Copy-Item $file $escalationFolder -Recurse -Force
            } else {
                # It's a file
                Copy-Item $file $escalationFolder -Force
            }
            Write-Host "âœ“ Added to escalation package: $(Split-Path $file -Leaf)" -ForegroundColor Green
        }
    }

    Write-Host "`nESCALATION PACKAGE READY AT: $escalationFolder" -ForegroundColor Yellow

service department for assistance. If the group is in your organization
and you don't know who the group owner is, you can find it by doing the
following in either Outlook on the web or Outlook: Open your Sent folder
and select the original message. If you're using Outlook on the web,
select the group name located on the To or CC line. If you're using
Outlook, double-click the group name located on the To or CC line. In
Outlook on the web, from the pop-up dialog box, choose Owner. In
Outlook, choose Contact. The owner's name is listed under Owner. The
owner of the group may have intentionally chosen to restrict who can
send messages to it, and they may not want to adjust the existing
restriction. In this case, you'll have to contact the group members by
some other means, such as sending an email message to their individual
email addresses or contacting them by phone. Was this helpful? Send

    # Federal Escalation Monitor with Response Tracking
    Add-Type -AssemblyName System.Speech
    $speech = New-Object System.Speech.Synthesis.SpeechSynthesizer

    Write-Host "FEDERAL ESCALATION MONITOR ACTIVATED" -ForegroundColor Green
    Write-Host "Tracking responses from 6 federal agencies" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    Write-Host "48-HOUR PROVINCIAL DEADLINE: $(Get-Date).AddHours(48)" -ForegroundColor Cyan

    $federalAgencies = @(
        "PPSC (Public Prosecution Service)",
        "CRCC (Civilian Review Commission)", 
        "CJC (Canadian Judicial Council)",
        "Public Safety Canada",
        "Department of Justice",
        "RCMP Ontario Operations"
    )

    $responseTracker = @()
    $deadline = (Get-Date).AddHours(48)

    while ($true) {
        $timeLeft = $deadline - (Get-Date)
        $hoursLeft = [math]::Round($timeLeft.TotalHours, 1)
        
        Write-Host "`n[$(Get-Date -Format 'HH:mm:ss')] Federal Monitor - $hoursLeft hours remaining" -ForegroundColor Magenta
        
        # Check for new email files
        $newFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads" -File | 
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-5) }
        
        if ($newFiles.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "ðŸš¨ $($newFiles.Count) NEW FILES DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($file in $newFiles) {
                $isFederal = $file.Name -match "federal|Federal|rcmp|RCMP|ppsc|PPSC|crc|CRC"
                $isGov = $file.Name -match "gov|Gov|gc\.ca|response|Response"
                
                Write-Host "  ðŸ“§ $($file.Name)" -ForegroundColor $(if($isFederal){"Green"}else{"Yellow"})
                
                if ($isFederal -or $isGov) {
                    Write-Host "    âš¡ FEDERAL/GOVERNMENT RESPONSE DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Green -BackgroundColor Black
                    $speech.SpeakAsync("Federal response received") | Out-Null
                    
                    # Archive to federal evidence
                    $federalPath = "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Federal_Responses"
                    if (!(Test-Path $federalPath)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $federalPath -Force }
                    Copy-Item $file.FullName "$federalPath\$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss')_$($file.Name)" -Force
                }
            }
        }
        
        # Check Gmail for new messages from federal domains
        Write-Host "  Monitoring federal domains: @gc.ca, @rcmp-grc.gc.ca, @justice.gc.ca" -ForegroundColor Gray
        
        # Alert based on time remaining
        if ($hoursLeft -le 24) {
            Write-Host "  âš  24-HOUR PROVINCIAL DEADLINE APPROACHING" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        }
        if ($hoursLeft -le 12) {
            Write-Host "  ðŸš¨ 12-HOUR WARNING - PREPARE FEDERAL ESCALATION" -ForegroundColor Red
        }
        if ($hoursLeft -le 6) {
            Write-Host "  ðŸš¨ðŸš¨ 6-HOUR CRITICAL - FEDERAL ESCALATION IMMINENT" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            $speech.SpeakAsync("Six hours until federal escalation") | Out-Null
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 60
    }

    # Enhanced response monitor with federal focus
    Write-Host "`nðŸ” ACTIVATING FEDERAL RESPONSE MONITOR..." -ForegroundColor Green

    while ($true) {
        $timestamp = Get-Date -Format "HH:mm:ss"
        
        # Check for new files with federal keywords
        $newFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path "$env:USERPROFILE\Downloads" -File | 
                    Where-Object { $_.LastWriteTime -gt (Get-Date).AddMinutes(-2) }
        
        $federalFiles = $newFiles | Where-Object { 
            $_.Name -match "federal|Federal|rcmp|RCMP|ppsc|PPSC|crc|CRC|gov|Gov|response|Response" 
        }
        
        if ($federalFiles.Count -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "`n" + "!"*70 -ForegroundColor Red
            Write-Host "[$timestamp] ðŸš¨ FEDERAL RESPONSE DETECTED!" -ForegroundColor Red -BackgroundColor White
            
            foreach ($file in $federalFiles) {
                Write-Host "   ðŸ“¬ $($file.Name)" -ForegroundColor Green
                Write-Host "   ðŸ“ Location: $($file.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
                Write-Host "   â° Modified: $($file.LastWriteTime)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
                
                # Immediate archive
                $federalArchive = "C:\Users\User\Desktop\Federal_Responses"
                if (!(Test-Path $federalArchive)) { New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $federalArchive -Force }
                $archivePath = "$federalArchive\$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss')_$($file.Name)"
                Copy-Item $file.FullName $archivePath -Force
                Write-Host "   ðŸ’¾ Archived: $archivePath" -ForegroundColor Magenta
            }
            
            Write-Host "!"*70 -ForegroundColor Red
            
            # Sound alert
            Add-Type -AssemblyName System.Speech
            $speech = New-Object System.Speech.Synthesis.SpeechSynthesizer
            $speech.SpeakAsync("Federal response received urgent") | Out-Null
        }
        else {
            Write-Host "[$timestamp] Monitoring federal responses..." -ForegroundColor Gray
        }
        
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 30
    }

to Fix It It appears you aren't in the same organization as the group
(or a sub-group) you're sending to or your email address isn't on the
group's allowed senders list. Ask the owner of the group to grant you
permission to send to it, and then try again. If the group belongs to a
different organization than yours, contact the organization's customer
service department for assistance. If the group is in your organization
and you don't know who the group owner is, you can find it by doing the
following in either Outlook on the web or Outlook: Open your Sent folder
and select the original message. If you're using Outlook on the web,
select the group name located on the To or CC line. If you're using
Outlook, double-click the group name located on the To or CC line. In
Outlook on the web, from the pop-up dialog box, choose Owner. In
Outlook, choose Contact. The owner's name is listed under Owner. The
owner of the group may have intentionally chosen to restrict who can
send messages to it, and they may not want to adjust the existing
restriction. In this case, you'll have to contact the group members by
some other means, such as sending an email message to their individual
email addresses or contacting them by phone. Was this helpful? Send

5.7.133 This error occurs when the distribution group, security group,

email admin or the group owner must add the sender's email address to
the group's allowed senders list or change the group's delivery
management setting to accept messages from senders inside and outside of
